
======================================================================
PAGE: Act 5

======================================================================

The fifth act of
Grim Dawn
is available only with the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion. It is set in the Forests north of
Burrwitch Village
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Act 6
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth, Locations
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Act_6
======================================================================

The sixth act of
Grim Dawn
is available only with the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion. It is set in the city of Malmouth.
Act 6 Quests

======================================================================
PAGE: Ashes of Malmouth
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Ashes_of_Malmouth
======================================================================

The
Ashes of Malmouth
is a content Expansion pack for
Grim Dawn
, released with the
v1.0.2.0
patch on October 11, 2017.
Ashes of Malmouth picks up where Grim Dawn leaves off, expanding the world and story with two new chapters in the epic struggle to free humankind from the horrors of the Aetherials. Deep within the fallen city of Malmouth, the Shaper of Flesh crafts grotesque living weapons that could deal a final blow to the human resistance. You must forge new alliances as you push forward through deep forest, the void and into the city itself in a heroic effort to end the Aetherial terror. Venture into dangerous new parts of the world as you discover unique items, empower your characters and make difficult choices that have a lasting impact on the people of Cairn.
Key Features
Level Cap Increased to 100
Increased Devotion cap of 55
Two New Masteries –
Inquisitor
and the
Necromancer
, both of which can be combined with the base game’s
Masteries
.
Two new Acts - Confront the devious
Aetherials
and their twisted abominations in the fallen city of
Malmouth
as you push forward alongside the
Black Legion
and
Inquisitor Creed
in two epic Chapters!
Transform Your Appearance – A brand-new
Illusionist
Service NPC enables you to transform the appearance of your equipment and customize your ideal look. Draw upon every item in your collection across all characters!
New Environments - Explore new parts of Cairn to the north of Burrwitch and beyond! Traverse the treacherous forest of Gloomwald and the murky Ugdenbog as you seek passage to the fallen city of Malmouth.
Four new
Factions
- New Factions provide more opportunities to make allies… and enemies. Earn their favor to unlock unique rewards, or become a nemesis to spawn powerful foes.
14 new
Constellations
- Unleash the might of the Arkovian Gods with 14 new Devotion Constellations that open up even more combinations in Grim Dawn’s massive constellation map.
Collect Hundreds of New
Items
- Dozens of new
Monster Infrequents
and Hundreds of
Epic and Legendary
items are waiting to be added to your collection! Combine them with the new Illusion System to create a look unique to you!
Item Skill Modifiers - Transmute and empower your Mastery skills using new modifiers found exclusively on equipment.
New Nemeses and Super Bosses - Tackle all-new vicious threats and earn their unique loot. Discover Cairn’s secrets to summon supremely powerful foes.
A New Rogue-Like Dungeon - A fourth Rogue-Like challenge dungeon, the
Ancient Grove
. Added shortly after release, it features the corrupting presence of the
Aetherials
and the
Chthonians
upon the beasts of
Cairn
.
Expanded Stash - Stow away precious treasure with a vastly expanded Personal Stash and an additional Shared Stash Tab.
Reset Your Attributes and Mastery Bar - Find a new type of
potion
that allows you reset your Attribute Points. Speak to a
Spirit Guide
to unlearn the Mastery Bar down to one point.
System Requirements
Minimum:
OS: Windows Vista / Windows 7 / Windows 8 / Windows 10
Processor: x86 compatible 2.3GHz or faster processor (Intel 2nd generation core i-series or equivalent)
Graphics: 512MB NVIDIA GeForce 6800 series or ATI Radeon X800 series or better
DirectX: Version 11
Storage: 2 GB available space
Sound Card: DirectX 11 compatible 16-bit sound card
Additional Notes: 4GB of memory is required to host multiplayer games

======================================================================
PAGE: Bladed Plating
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Bladed_Plating
======================================================================

Bladed Plating is a
component
for use in all
Armor
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Bladed Plating
"Armor plated fitted with rows of deadly blades. A favorite amongst brigands and ruthless tyrants."
(Used in all armor)
Component
+120
Health
+24
Offensive Ability
+30%
to All Retaliation Damage
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Bladed Plating Component.
Ugdenbloom
(8)
Ballistic Plating
(4)
Spined Carapace
(4)

Blazing Ruby is a
component
for use in
Amulets
and
Medals
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.

Health

15%

to All Retaliation

Item Level: 75

======================================================================
PAGE: Bloodied Crystal
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Bloodied_Crystal
======================================================================

Bloodied Crystal is a
component
for use in
Rings
,
Amulets
and
Medals
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint. The blueprint is a rare
Ashes of Malmouth
DLC loot drop that needs to be farmed.
Stats
Bloodied Crystal
"The once pearl-white crystal has absorbed unspeakable bloodshed.""
(Used in rings, amulets and medals)
Component
+40
Defensive Ability
15%
Bleeding Resistance
+75
Armor
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Bloodied Crystal Component.

(8)

(4)

The Conclave of the Three is an area in
Act 7
, and the main town and quest hub for
Forgotten Gods
Expansion content.

, leads to the

Crucible of the Dead
Location Info
Act:
6
Monster

n/a

n/a

Adjacent:
Edge of Reality

none
The Crucible of the Dead is a
secret area
in
Act 6
.
The area is a hidden easter-egg on Ultimate difficulty only, and is accessed by completing
Lokarr's Secret Quest
.

component

and

(Passive bonus)

+10%
Total Speed

Item Level: 75

======================================================================
PAGE: Forgotten Gods
CATEGORIES: Forgotten Gods
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Forgotten_Gods
======================================================================

Forgotten Gods
is the second content Expansion pack for
Grim Dawn
, released on March 27, 2019. It requires the
Ashes of Malmouth
Expansion to play.
In the Forgotten Gods expansion, the player will journey beyond the bounds of the Erulan Empire, traversing burning sands, lush oases and volcanic wastes to reach the sun beaten ruins of a city with secrets that should never have been disturbed. The flames of a forgotten god have been rekindled, sending ripples through the Eldritch realm and sowing terror even among the
Witch Gods
themselves.
Key Features
A brand new game mode -
The Shattered Realm
. Make your way through endless and ever more challenging maps to Earn unique rewards and mountains of loot.
A new Mastery - the
Oathkeeper
.
Additional skill/attribute points
Mobility Skills - available through
Rune Augments
, a new category of enchantments applied to
Medals
.
A massive new
story chapter
with new environments.
Difficulty Merits - after unlocking Elite or Ultimate difficulty, Merits can be purchased from a vendor in Forgotten Gods to allow new characters to skip Elite and/or Ultimate.
Transmutation - Visit the
Inventor
to reroll your duplicate
Set Items
to create new Set Pieces from the same set or entirely different sets.
Four new
Factions
.
Nine new
Constellations
.
The ability to transfer Iron between characters.  Iron bars can be purchased then placed in the transfer stash to be used by another character.
Hundreds of new Items - Dozens of new
Monster Infrequents
and Hundreds of
Epic and Legendary
items, including 12 new sets. including one  exclusive to the game's
Roguelike
dungeons and another to the Shattered Realm!
Expanded Stash - Forgotten Gods adds an additional Personal and Transfer Stash Tab.
Dozens of new enemy
creatures
, Bosses, and a new Nemesis.

======================================================================
PAGE: Living Armor
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Living_Armor
======================================================================

Living Armor is a Rare
component
for use in
Head Armor
,
Shoulder Armor
and
Chest Armor
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Living Armor
"The armor plate is more flesh than metal now as it writhes within your hands, clearly by the manipulation of Aetherials."
(Used in shoulder, chest and head armor)
Rare Component
+35
Offensive Ability
8%
Chaos Resistance
10%
Elemental Resistance
Increases Armor Absorption by
12%
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Living Armor Component.
Ugdenbloom
(16)
Ancient Armor Plate
(4)
Rotten Heart
(4)
Mutagenic Ichor
(4)

Runebound Topaz is a
component
for use in
Rings
,
Amulets
and
Medals
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Runebound Topaz
"A rune emblazoned upon the side of this gem empowers it with protective properties."
(Used in rings, amulets and medals)
Component
+160
Health
+52
Defensive Ability
10%
Reduced Stun Duration
+8%
Shield Damage Blocked
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Runebound Topaz Component.

Sacred Plating is a Rare
component
for use in
Head Armor
,
Shoulder Armor
and
Chest Armor
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Sacred Plating
"Plating from a once mighty set of armor, rumored to be blessed by Empyrion himself."
(Used in shoulder, chest and head armor)
Rare Component
+210
Health
14%
Vitality Resistance
18%
Aether Resistance
Increases Armor Absorption by
12%
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Sacred Plating Component.

Seal of Ancestry is a Rare
component
for use in
Amulets
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Seal of Ancestry
"The arcane seal evokes memories of your ancestors, even ones whom you never could have met in life."
(Used in amulets)
Rare Component
+5%
Health
+1.5
Energy Regenerated per second
Increases Energy Regeneration by
10%
10%
Vitality Resistance
Granted Skills
Ancestral Ward (Granted by Item)
The power within the seal shields you from the powers beyond.
100%
Chance of Activating
16
Second Skill Recharge
9000
Damage Absorption
Protects Against:
Aether
Chaos
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Seal of Ancestry Component.

Seal of Annihilation is a Rare
component
for use in
Amulets
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Seal of Annihilation
"A locus for the arcane flows of the universe."
(Used in amulets)
Rare Component
+20
Spirit
+5%
Attack Speed
+5%
Casting Speed
-10%
Skill Energy Cost
Granted Skills
Annihilation (15% Chance on Critical Attack)
The power within the seal annihilates your foe.
1
Second Skill Recharge
20%
Reduction to Enemy's Health
-55
Offensive Ability
-55
Defensive Ability
Increases Health Regeneration by
-50%
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Seal of Annihilation Component.

Seal of Blades is a
component
for use in all
Weapons
,
Shields
and caster
Off-Hands
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Seal of Blades
"The seal, devised by the legendary nightblade Belgothian, amplified the assassin's already deadly attacks and stimulated bleeding in the target."
(Used in all weapons, shields and caster off-hands)
Component
10
Piercing Damage
5%
of Attack Damage converted to Health
30
Bleeding Damage over
3
Seconds
+50%
Bleeding Damage
+50%
Pierce Damage
Granted Skills
Whirling Blades (Granted by Item)
At your command, whirling blades spin around you, shredding all foes who come too near.
This ability must be toggled to maintain its effect.
5
Meter Radius
155
Piercing Damage
145
Bleeding Damage per Second
15%

8%

Item Level: 75

Seal of Might is a
component
for use in all
Weapons
,
Shields
and caster
Off-Hands
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Seal of Might
"The seal, emblazoned by Ulgard the Mighty, focused the creator's considerable arcane power into unmatched physical might."
(Used in all weapons, shields and caster off-hands)
Component
13
Physical Damage
+50%

+50%

25%

+160
Health

This ability must be toggled to maintain its effect.

Seal of Skies is a
component
for use in all
Weapons
,
Shields
and caster
Off-Hands
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Seal of Skies
"The seal, first emblazoned by the arcane master Trozan, calls forth power from the celestial skies themselves."
(Used in all weapons, shields and caster off-hands)
Component
8-13
Lightning Damage
+50%

+50%
Lightning Damage
+50%

+50%

10%

+4%

Granted Skills
Chain Lightning (Granted by Item)
Lightning crackles at your fingertips and cascades off of your foes to demolish their ranks.

Energy Cost

3
targets
70%

235

176-425

300

2
Seconds

Can activate with all default weapon attacks.

PAGE: Spellscorched Plating
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Spellscorched_Plating
======================================================================

Spellscorched Plating is a
component
for use in all
Armor
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Spellscorched Plating
"Remnants of armor that survived a deadly arcane attack; the magical energies appear to be trapped within the metal."
(Used in all armor)
Component
+100
Health
20%
Pierce Resistance
15%
Elemental Resistance
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Spellscorched Plating Component.
Ugdenbloom
(8)
Resilient Plating
(4)
Runestone
(4)

======================================================================
PAGE: The Shattered Realm
CATEGORIES: Forgotten Gods
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/The_Shattered_Realm
======================================================================

The
Shattered Realm
is an endless dungeon introduced with the
Forgotten Gods
Expansion, and can be accessed by speaking to
Mazaan, Keeper of Portals
in the
Conclave of the Three
.
The Realm contains 73 custom levels, which load randomly. Levels are grouped into
Shards
. A Shard consists of three levels, or
Chunks
, plus a Boss level. Difficulty increases with each successive Shard, until the player chooses to end the session and claim the reward. The further one has progressed in the Shattered Realm, the greater the loot to be collected at the end.
Timer
Each Chunk has a progress bar, which is filled by killing enemies and collecting
Shattered Souls
. When the bar is full, the portal to the next Chunk opens. Completion of each Shard is subject to a countdown timer, and exceeding the timer will lessen the amount of loot collected at the end of the game session.
Shattered Souls
Common and Champion enemies have a small chance to drop
Shattered Soul
items, and Heroes and Nemesis foes will drop a
Greater Shattered Soul
.
Shattered Souls grant additional progress, and also give bonus damage and toughness for a period of 18 seconds. These buffs stack like charges, and each new Shattered Soul refreshes the duration.
Name
stack size
Shattered Soul
5
Mighty Shattered Soul
8
Celestial Shattered Soul
10
Overwhelming Shattered Soul
12
Shattered Soul charges last for 18 seconds and offer the following buffs:
Charge Level

96
Waystones
Waystones allow the player to enter the Shattered Realm at a particular Shard level. Blueprints can drop from one of the chests in the treasure room after completing a Shard level opened by the particular Waystone. They can then be crafted and given to
Mazaan
.
Shattered Waystone
Opens the way to at least the 2nd shard, up to the 6th shard.
Resonating Waystone
Opens the way to at least the 8th shard, up to the 12th shard.
Haunted Waystone
Opens the way to at least the 14th shard, up to the 18th shard.
Desecrated Waystone
Opens the way to at least the 20th shard, up to the 24th shard.
Celestial Waystone
Opens the way to at least the 26th shard, up to the 30th shard.
Eternal Waystone
Opens the way to at least the 32nd shard, up to the 36th shard.
Death's Waystone
Opens the way to at least the 38th shard, and beyond.
Rewards
At the end of each Shard, the player has the option to either continue or collect a reward. (A reward can also be collected after dying.) The Shattered Realm offers several unique items, including blueprints for Legendary
Rune Augments
and the level 94
Shattered Guardian
item
Set
.
Shattered Guardian Set pieces can be purchased from
Ullana, Shattered Squire
, the merchant in the Shattered Realm treasure room, upon reaching the appropriate levels as described in the table below. These set pieces are only available after completing a minimum of two shards.
Set Piece
Shard #
Cost (Iron)
Shattered Realm Armor
8?
100,000
Shattered Realm Ward
14?
140,000
Shattered Realm Mantle
18?
100,000
Shattered Realm Mask
24?
100,000
Note that the timer does not exclude you from these exclusive rewards.
New Shard level for shattered realm gear (after the shard squish) is a guess based on equivalent waystone levels.
Shrines
The Shattered Realm features several unique shrines, where rare
crafting materials
can be offered in exchange for specific buffs that come with a trade-off, similar to Mutators. These effects have a  50 minute duration and are applied to pets at a reduced rate.
Name
(Color) Description
Offering
Stats
Shrine of Azrakaa
(Yellow) Make a pact with Azrakaa, granting you Increased Resistance to Slow and Crowd Control effects, but your Critical Strikes are Weakened.

+60% Stun Resistance

+80% Total Speed Reduction Resistance

+33% to All Damage
-8% Physical Resistance
Shrine of Rattosh
(Green) Split your soul between this reality and the one beyond the veil, granting you Increased Resistance against All Damage, but your Health is reduced.

+10% Physical Resistance
+30% to all other resistances

+25/300/600 Armor

======================================================================
PAGE: Titan Plating
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Titan_Plating
======================================================================

Titan Plating is a Rare
component
for use in
Head Armor
and
Chest Armor
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Titan Plating
"An incredibly thick armor plating. The full set must have weighed more than any normal man could ever bear and still be able to move."
(Used in chest and head armor)
Rare Component
+4%
Physique
24%
Pierce Resistance
+33%
Reflected Damage Reduction
Increases Armor by
12%
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Titan Plating Component.
Ugdenbloom
(16)
Ancient Armor Plate
(4)
Imbued Silver
(4)
Frozen Heart
(4)

======================================================================
PAGE: Ugdenbog Leather
CATEGORIES: Ashes of Malmouth
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Ugdenbog_Leather
======================================================================

Ugdenbog Leather is a
component
for use in all
Armor
.
This item can be crafted after finding the Blueprint.
Stats
Ugdenbog Leather
"Leather from the beasts inhabiting the region known as Ugdenbog. The bog's deadly properties create some of the toughests beasts ever to roam Cairn."
(Used in all armor)
Component
+30
Defensive Ability
20%
Poison & Acid Resistance
20%
Bleeding Resistance
Required Player Level: 75
Item Level: 75
Blueprint
Crafts one complete Ugdenbog Leather Component.
Ugdenbloom
(8)
Antivenom Salve
(4)
Mutated Scales
(4)
Masteries
